############################################################################################################################
# 
# Generic Flavor Events - VIETmisc.0000-VIETmisc.0999 reserved
# Fired from the on_actions for every one, two, five, and ten years depending on rarity
# 
# Note to self:
# 
# is_available_at_peace_adult = yes <-- use as trigger if needed
# on_actions also has triggers
# has_game_rule = VIET_all_events / VIET_serious_events / VIET_balanced_events
# has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events / VIET_historical_universe_events / VIET_conversion_universe_events
# 
# base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
# content = minor_stress_impact_loss
# calm = medium_stress_impact_loss
# 
# Animations: idle, chancellor, steward, marshal, spymaster, chaplain, anger, rage, disapproval, disbelief, disgust, fear, sadness, shame, shock, worry, boredom, grief, paranoia, dismissal, flirtation, flirtation_left, love, schadenfreude, stress, happiness, ecstasy, admiration, lunatic (?), scheme, beg, pain, newborn, sick, severelywounded, prisonhouse, prisondungeon, war_attacker, war_defender, war_over_tie, war_over_win, war_over_loss, pregnant, personality_honorable, personality_dishonorable, personality_bold, personality_coward, personality_greedy, personality_content, personality_vengeful, personality_forgiving, personality_rational, personality_irrational, personality_compassionate, personality_callous, personality_zealous, personality_cynical

# GENERIC 0001-0046

# Character hears a bard sing Scarborough Fair
VIETmisc.0001 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0001.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0001.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = happiness
	}	

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_heard_Scarborough_Fair_event_happened }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_touching_moment 
	}
	
	option = { # Bravo!
		name = VIETmisc.0001.a
		add_stress = -50
		add_character_flag = VIET_heard_Scarborough_Fair_event_happened
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_heard_about_Scarborough_Fair
			days = 3650
		}		
	}
}


# Character dreams of going to a village in Oblivion
VIETmisc.0002 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0002.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0002.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_oblivion_pastoral_dream
	
	right_portrait = root	

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_character_modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_pells_gate
			has_character_modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_odiil_farm
			has_character_modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_weye
			has_character_modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_faregyl
			has_character_modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_cloud_ruler_temple
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Pell's Gate - forest town
		name = VIETmisc.0002.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_pells_gate
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Odiil Farm - fight off monsters
		name = VIETmisc.0002.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_odiil_farm
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Weye - fishing village
		name = VIETmisc.0002.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_weye
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Faregyl Inn - inn with breadmaker
		name = VIETmisc.0002.d
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_faregyl
			days = 1095
		}		
	}	
	option = { # Cloud Ruler Temple - ancient mountain temple
		name = VIETmisc.0002.e
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_oblivion_dream_cloud_ruler_temple
			days = 1095
		}		
	}
}

# Overhear an Oblivion conversation
VIETmisc.0004 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0004.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0004.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { event_background = corridor_day }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = boredom
	}
	

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Do something else
		name = VIETmisc.0004.a
		add_stress = -5
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_loss
			gregarious = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Talk with them
		name = VIETmisc.0004.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_overheard_oblivion_conversation
			days = 365
		}
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}
}



# Tried and failed to remember a dream
VIETmisc.0005 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0005.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0005.desc.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0005.desc
		}
	}
	theme = friendly
	override_background = {
		event_background = bedchamber
	}
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Oh well
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0005.a
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0005.a.norse
		}
		stress_impact = {
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}	
	}	
	option = { # Must remember!
		name = VIETmisc.0005.b
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0005.a.a
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0005.toast.a
					VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
				}
			}
			60 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0005.a.b
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0005.toast.b
					stress_impact = {
						base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
						stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Servant's child recently died
VIETmisc.0007 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0007.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0007.desc.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0007.desc
		}
	}
	theme = family
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Say generic words of condolence
		name = VIETmisc.0007.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_compassion = 1
			}
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Religious option
		name = VIETmisc.0007.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_zeal = 1
			}
		}
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # I don't care
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0007.c
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0007.c.norse
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_compassion = -1
			}
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Give servant a couple weeks off
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0007.d
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0007.d.norse
		}
		trigger = {
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		trait = compassionate
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_compassion = 1
			}
		}
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_tiny_prestige_loss_effect = yes
	}
}

# Legs get numb while sitting on the chamber pot
VIETmisc.0010 = {
	type = character_event
	title = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0010.t.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0010.t
		}
	}
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0010.desc.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0010.desc
		}
	}
	theme = secret
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = stress
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Call for help
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0010.a
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0010.a.norse
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_rationality = 100
			}
		}
		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Try to stand by self
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0010.b
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0010.b.norse
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_zeal = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					desc = VIETmisc.0010.b.a.norse
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_good
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0010.toast.b.fall.norse
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0010.toast.b.fall.norse
					}
				}
				60 = {
					desc = VIETmisc.0010.b.b.norse
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0010.toast.b.norse
						increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = fall }
						VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					desc = VIETmisc.0010.b.a
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_good
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0010.toast.a
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0010.toast.b.fall
					}
				}
				60 = {
					desc = VIETmisc.0010.b.b
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0010.toast.b
						increase_wounds_no_death_effect = { REASON = fall }
						VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}		
		}
	}
}

# Reports of a ghost in residence
VIETmisc.0012 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0012.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0012.desc.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0012.desc
		}
	}
	theme = secret
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = paranoia
	}  
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1

		}

		}

# Meeting a foreign envoy when you can't hold your bladder
VIETmisc.0023 = {
	type = character_event
	title = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0023.t.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0023.t
		}
	}
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0023.desc.norse
			}
			desc = VIETmisc.0023.desc
		}
	}
	theme = crown
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = pain
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		play_music_cue = mx_cue_stress 
	}
	
	option = { # Run to the chamber pot immediately
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0023.a
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0023.a.norse
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		VIET_random_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
	}	
	
	option = { # Try to hold it in
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = no }
			text = VIETmisc.0023.b
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes }
			text = VIETmisc.0023.b.norse
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIET_norse_localization_trigger = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				# Successfully hold it in until the dignitary is done
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = calm
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = stubborn
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = patient
					}
					desc = VIETmisc.0023.b.a.norse
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_good
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.success.title.norse
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.success.norse
						stress_impact = {
							base = minor_stress_impact_gain
						}
					}			
				}
				# Fail to hold it in until the dignitary is done
				70 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = paranoid
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = impatient
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = fickle
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = shy
					}
					desc = VIETmisc.0023.b.b.norse
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.failure.title.norse
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.failure.norse
						VIET_random_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
						stress_impact = {
							base = medium_stress_impact_gain
						}
					}			
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				# Successfully hold it in until the dignitary is done
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = calm
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = stubborn
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = patient
					}
					desc = VIETmisc.0023.b.a
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_good
						left_icon = ROOT
						title = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.success.title
						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.success
						stress_impact = {
							base = minor_stress_impact_gain
						}
					}			
				}
				# Fail to hold it in until the dignitary is done
				70 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = paranoid
					}

						add = 10
						has_trait = impatient
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = fickle
					}
					modifier = {
						add = 10
						has_trait = shy
					}
					desc = VIETmisc.0023.b.b
					send_interface_toast = {
						type = event_toast_effect_bad
						left_icon = ROOT

						custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0023.toast.b.failure
						VIET_random_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
						stress_impact = {
							base = medium_stress_impact_gain
						}
					}			
				}
			}		
		}
	}

		}

# Courtier bumps into you accidentally
VIETmisc.0041 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0041.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0041.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	override_background = { event_background = garden }
	
	left_portrait = { 	
		character = scope:scope_VIET_slip_bumper
		animation = fear
	}	
	right_portrait = { 	
		character = root
		animation = anger
	}
	

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_serious_events }
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_slip_bumper
		}
	}
	
	option = { # be polite
		name = VIETmisc.0041.a
		scope:scope_VIET_slip_bumper = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_get_angry
			}		
		}
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # be a jerk
		name = VIETmisc.0041.b
		scope:scope_VIET_slip_bumper = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_angry_at_me
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_bumped_into_me
			}			
		}
		add_dread = minor_dread_gain
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

		name = VIETmisc.0043.a

				desc = VIETmisc.0043.a.a
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_bad
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0043.toast.a
					custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0043.toast.failure
					VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
					add_stress = 10
				}			
			}
			50 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0043.a.b
				send_interface_toast = {
					type = event_toast_effect_good
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0043.toast.b
					custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0043.toast.success
					VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # skillfully avoid their name
		name = VIETmisc.0043.b
		add_stress = 5
		random = {
			chance = 33
			VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Curl up with a good book?
VIETmisc.0047 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0047.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0047.desc
	theme = learning
	override_background = { event_background = sitting_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	

	trigger = {
		learning >= medium_skill_rating
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
	}
	
	option = { # read
		name = VIETmisc.0047.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = diligent
					has_trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
				ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		else = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_loss
				shy = major_stress_impact_loss
			}		
		}
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_curled_up_with_good_book
			years = 5
		}
	}	
	option = { # don't get too into it
		name = VIETmisc.0047.b
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}		
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_curled_up_with_good_book
			years = 1
		}
	}
}



# Actors in a play are too melodramatic and suck at acting
VIETmisc.0048 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0048.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0048.desc

	override_background = { event_background = market }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Waste!
		name = VIETmisc.0048.a
	}	
	option = { # Give money out of pity
		name = VIETmisc.0048.b
		trigger = {
			has_trait = generous
		}
		trait = generous
		remove_short_term_gold = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			generous = minor_stress_impact_loss
			wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Lash them
		name = VIETmisc.0048.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = sadistic
		}
		trait = sadistic
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate					
						trait_is_virtue = patient					
						trait_is_virtue = calm					
						trait_is_virtue = forgiving					
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 5
		stress_impact = {
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
	}	
	option = { # Give them advice
		name = VIETmisc.0048.d
		trigger = {
			diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = diplomacy
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_constructive_criticism
			days = 730
		}
	}	
	option = { # Horny option
		name = { # Into women
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_female = no
						NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
					}
					AND = {
						is_female = yes
						OR = {
							has_sexuality = homosexual						
							has_sexuality = bisexual						
						}
					}
				}
			}
			text = VIETmisc.0048.e
		}
		name = { # Into men
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_female = yes
						NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
					}
					AND = {
						is_female = no
						OR = {
							has_sexuality = homosexual						
							has_sexuality = bisexual						
						}
					}
				}
			}
			text = VIETmisc.0048.f
		}
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = celibate
				has_sexuality = asexual
			}			
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lustful_ruler
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

	}

		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0052.a
		random_list = {
			20 = { VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes }
			10 = { VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes }
		}
	}	
	option = { # horny option
		name = VIETmisc.0052.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = celibate
				has_sexuality = asexual
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = { has_sexuality = homosexual }
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					OR = {
						has_sexuality = homosexual						
						has_sexuality = bisexual						
					}
				}
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = minor_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = minor_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lustful_ruler
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

# Courtier is haunted by a ghost that tells them to repent for their sins
VIETmisc.0061 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0061.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0061.desc
	theme = secret
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_callous
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner
		animation = fear
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			num_sinful_traits >= 1
			num_virtuous_traits <= 1
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				num_sinful_traits >= 1
				num_virtuous_traits <= 1
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_haunted_sinner
		}
	}
	
	option = { # pray
		name = VIETmisc.0061.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_haunted_by_ghost_for_sin
				years = 3
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_prayed_for_me
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner
			OPINION = no
		}
	}	
	option = { # reform!
		name = VIETmisc.0061.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_haunted_by_ghost_for_sin
				years = 3
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_nagged_me
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
	option = { # not my problem
		name = VIETmisc.0061.c
		add_dread = 10
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_haunted_by_ghost_for_sin
				years = 6
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_care_about_me
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
	option = { # liar
		name = VIETmisc.0061.d
		add_dread = 10
		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = minor_stress_impact_loss
			trusting = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_haunted_by_ghost_for_sin
				years = 6
			}
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_doesnt_care_about_me
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_haunted_sinner
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
}

				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_hell_wonderer
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Hot hell
		name = VIETmisc.0062.a
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_hell_wonderer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Cold hell
		name = VIETmisc.0062.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_hell_wonderer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Don't talk
		name = VIETmisc.0062.c
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_dread = 3
		scope:scope_VIET_hell_wonderer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_nagged_me
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Focus on living good lives
		name = VIETmisc.0062.d
		VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_hell_wonderer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Cynical option
		name = VIETmisc.0062.e
		trigger = {
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		trait = cynical
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			craven = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_hell_wonderer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_interesting_conversation
			}		
		}
	}
}

# You and a courtier find a lost child
VIETmisc.0064 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0064.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0064.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	right_portrait = scope:scope_VIET_child_sob_help
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
				has_trait = humble
				has_trait = patient
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = callous
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = just
					has_trait = humble
					has_trait = patient
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = callous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_child_sob_help
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Go ahead without me
		name = VIETmisc.0064.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Let's find the parents together
		name = VIETmisc.0064.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_honor = 1
				ai_compassion = 1
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_child_sob_help = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_mutual_compassion
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_mutual_compassion
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_child_sob_help
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
	option = { # Who cares about the child
		name = VIETmisc.0064.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			ai_value_modifier = {
				ai_honor = -1
				ai_compassion = -1
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_child_sob_help = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_ignored_child
			}	
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_child_sob_help
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
}

			days = 1095
		}
	}	
	option = { # I'm a nerd

		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = learning
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_impressed_others_with_knowledge
			days = 365
		}
	}
}



# Visiting scholar recommends making some changes to your house for fire safety reasons

			has_trait = gregarious
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
	}

				gold >= 25

			}
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_house_fire_safety_measures
			days = 3650
		}

				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on

			limit = {
				gold >= 25
			}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0077.info
		}
	}	
	option = { # He's up to something!

		}

		add_dread = 5

			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0077.info
		}
	}
}

# Baklava merchant offers special baklava
VIETmisc.0079 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0079.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0079.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	override_background = { event_background = market }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		VIET_is_baklava_culture_trigger = yes
		gold >= 10
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Normal baklava
		name = VIETmisc.0079.a
		remove_short_term_gold = 10
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_normal
			days = 365
		}
	}	
	option = { # Baklava w/ cheese
		name = VIETmisc.0079.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 20
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_sweet_cheese
			days = 365
		}
	}	
	option = { # Baklava w/ spices
		name = VIETmisc.0079.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 20
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_spices
			days = 365
		}
	}	
	option = { # Baklava w/ fruits
		name = VIETmisc.0079.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 20
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 20
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_fruits
			days = 365
		}
	}	
	option = { # All the baklava!!!
		name = VIETmisc.0079.e
		trigger = {
			has_trait = gluttonous
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 60
			}
		}
		trait = gluttonous
		remove_short_term_gold = 60
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_normal
			days = 365
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_sweet_cheese
			days = 365
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_spices
			days = 365
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_bought_baklava_fruits
			days = 365
		}
	}
}



# A courtier is obsessed with baklava
VIETmisc.0080 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0080.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0080.desc
	theme = feast_activity
	override_background = { event_background = throne_room }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_forgiving
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_baklava_fanatic
		animation = personality_greedy
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		VIET_is_baklava_culture_trigger = yes
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			VIET_is_baklava_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				VIET_is_baklava_culture_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_baklava_fanatic
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Very funny!
		name = VIETmisc.0080.a
		scope:scope_VIET_baklava_fanatic = {
			VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_baklava_fanatic
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # I like it too
		name = VIETmisc.0080.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_baklava_fanatic
			years = 10
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_baklava_fanatic = {
			VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_baklava_fanatic
				years = 10
			}
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_baklava_fanatic
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		base = 1

			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}

			add = 0.2

		}

		}

			add = -0.2

		}

		scope:scope_VIET_baklava_gifter = {

		}
	}

		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_baklava_donate_to_poor
			years = 4

		}

# Farmer tried to cheat a deal by altering the tally sticks but is caught
VIETmisc.0087 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0087.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0087.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_callous
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Let him go
		name = VIETmisc.0087.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = forgiving
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0087.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Make him pay a fine
		name = VIETmisc.0087.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0087.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Imprison him
		name = VIETmisc.0087.c
		add_dread = 7
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0087.info
		}
	}	
}



# Gambling with loaded dice in the market
VIETmisc.0088 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0088.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0088.desc
	theme = family
	override_background = { event_background = market }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = generous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Won't gamble
		name = VIETmisc.0088.a		
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = greedy
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = temperate
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Gamble a bit
		name = VIETmisc.0088.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 0
			}
			intrigue < decent_skill_rating
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_sin = greedy
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 10
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 16
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 25
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0088.win.small
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0088.win.small
					random_list = {
						40 = { add_gold = 10 }
						30 = { add_gold = 20 }
						20 = { add_gold = 30 }
						10 = { add_gold = 40 }
					}
				}
			}
			80 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0088.lose.small
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0088.lose.small
					stress_impact = {
						base = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 10 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 15 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 20 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 25 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Gamble a lot
		name = VIETmisc.0088.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 0
			}
			intrigue < decent_skill_rating
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_sin = greedy
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 10
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 16
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 25
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0088.win.big
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0088.win.big
					random_list = {
						40 = { add_gold = 25 }
						30 = { add_gold = 35 }
						20 = { add_gold = 45 }
						10 = { add_gold = 55 }
					}
				}
			}
			80 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0088.lose.big
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0088.lose.big
					stress_impact = {
						base = minor_stress_impact_gain
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 25 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 30 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 35 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 40 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # He's using weighted dice!
		name = VIETmisc.0088.d
		trigger = {
			intrigue >= decent_skill_rating
		}
		skill = intrigue
		VIET_large_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Will manipulate things against him
		name = VIETmisc.0088.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				gold >= 0
			}
			intrigue >= decent_skill_rating
		}
		skill = intrigue	
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_sin = greedy
				}
			}
			VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 15
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 20
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 7
					intrigue >= 25
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0088.win.big
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0088.win.big
					random_list = {
						40 = { add_gold = 25 }
						30 = { add_gold = 35 }
						20 = { add_gold = 45 }
						10 = { add_gold = 55 }
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				desc = VIETmisc.0088.lose.small
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0088.lose.small
					stress_impact = {

						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 20 }

					}

		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {

		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2

		}
	}

	
	option = { # Okay Anakin

		}
	}	
}




# See an earthworm on the road
VIETmisc.0090 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0090.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0090.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Do nothing
		name = VIETmisc.0090.a
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Help it
		name = VIETmisc.0090.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = patient
						trait_is_virtue = calm
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}		
	option = { # Kill it
		name = VIETmisc.0090.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = patient
						trait_is_virtue = calm
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 5
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
}



# Find what appears to be an ancient skeleton buried near a construction site
VIETmisc.0091 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0091.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0091.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	right_portrait = root
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			10 = { add_character_flag = VIET_skeleton_found_intrigue_reality }
			10 = { add_character_flag = VIET_skeleton_found_learning_reality }
		}
	}

	
	option = { # It's just a skeleton
		name = VIETmisc.0091.a
		VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = minor_stress_impact_gain
			just = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Bury it
		name = VIETmisc.0091.b
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
	}	
	option = { # Skeleton is actually a recent murder victim!
		name = VIETmisc.0091.c
		trigger = {
			intrigue >= medium_skill_rating
			has_character_flag = VIET_skeleton_found_intrigue_reality
		}
		skill = intrigue
		custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0091.c.tooltip
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_intrigue_lifestyle_xp = medium_lifestyle_xp
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_helped_solve_old_murder_mystery
			years = 8
		}
	}	
	option = { # Skeleton should be studied
		name = VIETmisc.0091.d
		trigger = {
			learning >= medium_skill_rating
			has_character_flag = VIET_skeleton_found_learning_reality
		}
		skill = learning
		custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0091.d.tooltip
		add_learning_lifestyle_xp = medium_lifestyle_xp
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_studying_ancient_clothes
			years = 8
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_character_flag = VIET_skeleton_found_intrigue_reality
		remove_character_flag = VIET_skeleton_found_learning_reality
	}
}

# Thunderstone Talisman - Thunderstones found near the area
VIETmisc.0094 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0094.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0094.desc
	theme = learning
	
	right_portrait = root
	artifact = { # To display the artifact in the event-window
		target = scope:VIET_clutter_artifact
		position = lower_center_portrait
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		# Reduce spam
		modifier = {
			add = -0.9
			any_character_artifact = {
				has_variable = VIET_thunderstone_talisman_variable
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.4
			VIET_has_2_clutter_artifacts_trigger = yes	
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.5
			VIET_has_4_clutter_artifacts_trigger = yes	
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	immediate = {	
		hidden_effect_new_artifact = {
			create_artifact = {
				name = VIET_thunderstone_talisman_name
				description = VIET_thunderstone_talisman_desc
				type = VIET_clutter
				visuals = VIET_thunderstone_talisman
				quality = 15
				wealth = 15
				modifier = artifact_VIET_thunderstone_talisman_modifier
				#max_durability = 40
				save_scope_as = VIET_clutter_artifact
				history = {
					type = created_before_history
				}
			}
			scope:VIET_clutter_artifact = {
				set_variable = VIET_thunderstone_talisman_variable
			}
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Give them to farmers
		name = VIETmisc.0094.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			destroy_artifact = scope:VIET_clutter_artifact
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0094.info
		}
	}	
	option = { # Give them to local temple
		name = VIETmisc.0094.b
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			destroy_artifact = scope:VIET_clutter_artifact
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0094.info
		}
	}	
	option = { # Use as charms to ward off bad luck
		name = VIETmisc.0094.c
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:VIET_clutter_artifact = {
				set_owner = {
					target = root
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = VIET_artifact_limit_warning
		# add_character_modifier = {
		# 	modifier = VIET_thunderstone_talisman
		# 	years = 8
		# }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0094.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Give to scholars to study
		name = VIETmisc.0094.d
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_thunderstone_studies
			years = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			destroy_artifact = scope:VIET_clutter_artifact
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0094.info
		}
	}

# Courtier dreams of the sandman
VIETmisc.0095 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0095.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0095.desc
	theme = vassal
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_sandman_dreamer
		animation = happiness
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_sandman_skeptic
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
		}	
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			has_trait = cynical
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_trait = cynical }
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_sandman_dreamer
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				has_trait = cynical
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_sandman_skeptic
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Dream is probably real
		name = VIETmisc.0095.a
		scope:scope_VIET_sandman_dreamer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_believed_sandman_story
			}		
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_sandman_skeptic = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_sandman_dialogue_disagree
			}		
		}
	}	
	option = { # Dream is probably just a dream
		name = VIETmisc.0095.b
		scope:scope_VIET_sandman_dreamer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_didnt_believe_sandman_story
			}		
		}

				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_sandman_dialogue_agree
			}		
		}
	}

# Courtier pranks another by pretending there's a ghost around
VIETmisc.0097 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0097.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0097.desc
	theme = friendly
	override_background = { event_background = corridor_day }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prankster
		animation = schadenfreude
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prank_victim
		animation = fear
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = deceitful
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = shy
				has_trait = craven
				has_trait = trusting					
				has_trait = paranoid					
			}
		}	
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = shy
				has_trait = craven
				has_trait = trusting
				has_trait = paranoid
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = deceitful
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = shy
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = trusting					
					has_trait = paranoid					
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_ghost_prankster
		}	
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = shy
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = trusting
					has_trait = paranoid
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_ghost_prank_victim
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Stop the pranking
		name = VIETmisc.0097.a
		scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prankster = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastised_ghost_pranker
			}		
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prank_victim = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_supported_ghost_prank_victim
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prank_victim
			OPINION = no
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prankster
			OPINION = no
		}
	}	
	option = { # Stop falling for pranks
		name = VIETmisc.0097.b
		scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prankster = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_supported_ghost_pranker
			}		
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prank_victim = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_chastised_ghost_prank_victim
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prankster
			OPINION = no
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_ghost_prank_victim
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
}



# Courtier pretends to be a ghost to scare off local kids
VIETmisc.0098 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0098.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0098.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_fake_ghost
		animation = anger
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			OR = {
				has_trait = wrathful
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = impatient
				has_trait = vengeful
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = shy
				has_trait = craven
				has_trait = compassionate					
				has_trait = forgiving					
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = wrathful
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = impatient
					has_trait = vengeful
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = shy
					has_trait = craven
					has_trait = compassionate					
					has_trait = forgiving					
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_fake_ghost
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Who cares
		name = VIETmisc.0098.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_scooby_doo_villain_let_go
			years = 4
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_fake_ghost = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_scooby_doo_villain_release
			}		
		}
		stress_impact = {
			just = medium_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}	
	option = { # Apologize to locals
		name = VIETmisc.0098.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_fake_ghost = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_scooby_doo_villain_forced_apology
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_fake_ghost
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
	option = { # Compensate locals
		name = VIETmisc.0098.c
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_scooby_doo_villain_punisher
			years = 4
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_fake_ghost = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_scooby_doo_villain_forced_reward
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_fake_ghost
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
}

		name = VIETmisc.0101.a
		add_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_nice

			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain

			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = VIETmisc.0102
	}
}


# Come across an unknown servant - is he a spirit testing one's hospitality?
VIETmisc.0102 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0102.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0102.desc
	theme = friendly
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = paranoia
	}
	
	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.0102.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_nice
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_hospitality_spirit_blessing
				years = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_mean
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_hospitality_spirit_cursed
				years = 4
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_nice
			}
			remove_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_nice
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_mean
			}
			remove_character_flag = VIET_spirit_character_test_mean
		}
	}
}

			NAND = {
				has_trait = zealous
				religion = religion:islam_religion
			}
			OR = {
				has_trait = gregarious
				has_trait = drunkard
				has_trait = lustful
				has_trait = lazy
				has_trait = trusting
				has_trait = gluttonous
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = temperate
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NAND = {
					has_trait = zealous
					religion = religion:islam_religion
				}
				OR = {
					has_trait = gregarious
					has_trait = drunkard
					has_trait = lustful
					has_trait = lazy
					has_trait = trusting
					has_trait = gluttonous
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_court_sleepy
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_bad_hangover
				years = 3
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Go home and rest
		name = VIETmisc.0107.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_court_sleepy = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_bad_hangover_break
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_court_sleepy
			OPINION = no
		}
	}
	option = { # Have some water
		name = VIETmisc.0107.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		scope:scope_VIET_court_sleepy = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_bad_hangover_relief
			}		
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_court_sleepy
			OPINION = no
		}		
	}
	option = { # Ha ha!
		name = VIETmisc.0107.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_amused_ruler
			days = 777
		}
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_court_sleepy = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_bad_hangover_mockery
			}		
		}		
	}
}

scripted_trigger VIETmisc0111_foreign_traveler_trigger = {
	is_adult = yes
	OR = {
		faith.religion = root.faith.religion
		culture = {
			has_same_culture_heritage = root.culture
		}
	}
}

scripted_trigger VIETmisc0111_foreign_ruler_for_creation_trigger = {
	in_diplomatic_range = root
	OR = {
		faith.religion = root.faith.religion
		culture = {
			has_same_culture_heritage = root.culture
		}
	}
}

scripted_effect VIETmisc0111_add_courtier_effect = {
	save_scope_as = new_courtier
	root = { add_courtier = scope:new_courtier }
	add_opinion = {
		target = root
		modifier = grateful_opinion
		opinion = $OPINION$
	}
}

# Come across an adventurer left for dead
VIETmisc.0111 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0111.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0111.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_skyrim_forest
	
	left_portrait = root
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
		animation = wounded
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_pool_character = {
				province = root.capital_province
				limit = { VIETmisc0111_foreign_traveler_trigger = yes }
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
			}

			#No such character? Let's make one
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { exists = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person } }

				random_independent_ruler = {
					limit = { VIETmisc0111_foreign_ruler_for_creation_trigger = yes }
					save_scope_as = creation_template_ruler
				}

				create_character = {
					location = root.capital_province
					template = pool_repopulate_prowess
					culture = scope:creation_template_ruler.culture
					faith = scope:creation_template_ruler.faith
					save_scope_as = scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { exists = scope:create_family_blocker }
						exists = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person # They will exist, but we do this to suppress errors for newly created characters not existing while trigger tooltips are generating
					}
					game_rule_create_spouse_and_children = { CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person } # They will exist, but we do this to suppress errors for newly created characters not existing while trigger tooltips are generating
				
				# Do they have a traveling family?
				scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person = {
					random_traveling_family_member = {
						limit = { is_spouse_of = prev }
						alternative_limit = { NOT = { this = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person } }
						save_scope_as = traveler_family_1
					}
					if = {
						limit = { exists = scope:traveler_family_1 }
						random_traveling_family_member = {
							limit = {
								NOR = {
									this = scope:traveler_family_1
									this = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
								}
							}
							save_scope_as = traveler_family_2
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { exists = scope:traveler_family_2 }
						random_traveling_family_member = {
							limit = {
								NOR = {
									this = scope:traveler_family_1
									this = scope:traveler_family_2
									this = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
								}
							}
							save_scope_as = traveler_family_3
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { exists = scope:traveler_family_3 }
						random_traveling_family_member = {
							limit = {
								NOR = {
									this = scope:traveler_family_1
									this = scope:traveler_family_2
									this = scope:traveler_family_3
									this = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
								}
							}
							save_scope_as = traveler_family_4
						}
					}
				}
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person = {
				increase_wounds_effect = {
					REASON = pilgrimage_bandit_attack
				}	
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_adventurer_left_for_dead_origin
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	option = { # Leave them be
		name = VIETmisc.0111.a
		VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		add_dread = 10
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = medium_stress_impact_gain
			generous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person = {
				random = {
					chance = 50
					death = {
						death_reason = death_wounds
					}	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Escort them to the safety of town
		name = VIETmisc.0111.b
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Invite them to court
		name = VIETmisc.0111.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 15
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person = {
			if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:traveler_family_1 }
				every_traveling_family_member = {
					#custom = yearly.1090.travelers_family
					VIETmisc0111_add_courtier_effect = { OPINION = 50 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				VIETmisc0111_add_courtier_effect = { OPINION = 50 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_add_hook = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
					type = loyalty_hook
				}
			}
			add_hook = {
				target = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
				type = loyalty_hook
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { can_set_relation_potential_friend_trigger = { CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person } }
				set_relation_potential_friend = scope:scope_VIET_left_for_dead_person
			}
		}
	}
}

# Smell a weird smell
VIETmisc.0112 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0112.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0112.desc
	theme = realm
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = paranoia
	}	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_no_smell_courtier
		animation = personality_cynical
	}
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier_or_guest = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_guest = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_no_smell_courtier
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # I smell it!
		name = VIETmisc.0112.a
		stress_impact = {
			fickle = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			deceitful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			trusting = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_smelling_smells
			days = 444
		}
	}	
	option = { # Take a rest
		name = VIETmisc.0112.b
		stress_impact = {
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			honest = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			shy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_smelling_smells
			days = 444
		}
	}
}

			add = -0.2

		}
		modifier = {

		}

			chance = 40

				add = -15				
				num_virtuous_traits >= 1
			}

				left_icon = ROOT
				title = VIETmisc.0115.toast
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = VIET_prison_ghost_curse
					years = 8
				}
			}
		}		
	}

# Witness a couple fornicating in public
VIETmisc.0116 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0116.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0116.desc
	theme = seduction
	override_background = { event_background = alley_day }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = shock
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Debauched commoners
		name = VIETmisc.0116.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_witnessed_public_fornication
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			humble = medium_stress_impact_gain
			lustful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0116.info
		}	
	}	
	option = { # Not one to judge
		name = VIETmisc.0116.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_witnessed_public_fornication
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0116.info
		}	
	}	
	option = { # Aroused ruler
		name = VIETmisc.0116.c
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_sexuality = asexual
				has_sexuality = homosexual # Witnessing a hetereosexual couple
				has_trait = celibate
				has_trait = eunuch
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_lustful_ruler
			years = 3
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_witnessed_public_fornication
			years = 3
		}
		stress_impact = {
			chaste = medium_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0116.info
		}	
	}	
	option = { # Join them
		name = VIETmisc.0116.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = lustful
			is_female = no
			OR = {
				gold >= 5
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 5
		trait = lustful
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_threesome_with_commoners
			years = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0116.info
		}	
	}
}

		}

# Come across an abandoned baby - what to do?
VIETmisc.0128 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0128.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0128.desc
	theme = family
	override_background = { event_background = VIET_background_skyrim_forest }
	
	left_portrait = root
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
		animation = newborn
	}
	
	#lower_center_portrait = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
	
	trigger = {
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
			NOT = { is_close_or_extended_family_of = root }
			is_married = no
			is_concubine = no
			OR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
				has_trait = generous
			}
			NOR = {
				has_trait = sadistic
				has_trait = callous
				has_trait = paranoid
				has_trait = wrathful
			}
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = wrathful
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
				NOT = { is_close_or_extended_family_of = root }
				is_married = no
				is_concubine = no
				OR = {
					has_trait = compassionate
					has_trait = just
					has_trait = generous
				}
				NOR = {
					has_trait = sadistic
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = paranoid
					has_trait = wrathful
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				location = root.capital_province
				age = { 1 2 }
				gender_female_chance = 50
				faith = root.faith
				culture = root.culture
				save_scope_as = scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
				random_traits = yes
			}
			# scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
			# 	add_character_modifier = {
			# 		modifier = VIET_abaonded_as_a_child
			# 	}
			# }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Leave it to die
		name = VIETmisc.0128.a
		add_dread = 20
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_abandoned_a_baby
			years = 10
		}
		scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
			add_opinion = {
				target = root
				modifier = VIET_opinion_abandoned_baby
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_trait = callous
					has_trait = sadistic
				}
			}
			stress_impact = {
				base = minor_stress_impact_gain
				compassionate = massive_stress_impact_gain
				just = medium_stress_impact_gain
				generous = medium_stress_impact_gain
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_wolves # Maybe something else in the future?
				}			
			}
		}
		progress_towards_rival_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
			OPINION = no
		}
	}		
	option = { # Let a servant adopt it
		name = VIETmisc.0128.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_saved_abandoned_baby
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = major_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				death = {
					death_reason = death_disappearance
				}			
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { # Let courtier adopt it
		name = VIETmisc.0128.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_virtue = compassionate
						trait_is_virtue = generous
						trait_is_virtue = just
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_large_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_saved_abandoned_baby
			years = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				set_mother = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer		
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
					is_female = no
				}
			}
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = {
				set_father = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer		
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#We take care of the sundries in a hidden effect so as not to put too much into the tooltip.
			scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby = { set_house = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer.house }
			add_courtier = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
			scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer = {
				add_opinion = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
					modifier = VIET_opinion_adopted_child
				}	
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					target = scope:scope_VIET_abandoned_baby
					modifier = VIET_opinion_adopted_parent
				}	
			}
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = major_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = medium_stress_impact_gain
			arbitrary = minor_stress_impact_gain
			greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}
		progress_towards_friend_effect = {
			CHARACTER = scope:scope_VIET_baby_rescuer
			OPINION = no
		}
	}	
}
