# Noble wants to hunt nilgai that is sacred to a village
VIETmisc.0217 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0217.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0217.desc
	theme = hunt_activity
	override_background = { event_background = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			any_county_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_burma
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0217.a
		stress_impact = {
			diligent = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0217.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0217.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_let_noble_hunt_nilgai
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			just = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0217.info
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0217.c
		VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_protected_sacred_nilgai
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0217.info
		}
	}
}

# Servant sees a parliament of rooks in your garden
VIETmisc.0221 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0221.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0221.desc
	theme = death
	override_background = { event_background = garden }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = worry
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = world_europe
				geographical_region = custom_outremer
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = world_steppe
				geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
			}
		}		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0221.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0221.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0221.b
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 40
				modifier = {
					add = 15
					num_sinful_traits >= 1
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -15				
					num_virtuous_traits >= 1
				}
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0221.b.tooltip
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = VIET_rook_curse
						years = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0221.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0221.c
		trigger = {
			VIET_is_crow_lord_or_lady_trigger = yes
		}
		VIET_large_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_large_piety_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_befriending_rooks
			years = 8
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0221.info
		}
	}
}

# Come across some hunters hunting chamois
VIETmisc.0224 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0224.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0224.desc
	theme = hunt_activity
	override_background = { event_background = VIET_background_skyrim_forest }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		capital_province = {
			OR = {
				geographical_region = special_cagot_region
				geographical_region = custom_burgundy
				geographical_region = world_europe_south_italy
				geographical_region = custom_bavaria
				geographical_region = custom_core_switzerland
				geographical_region = world_europe_south_east
				geographical_region = world_asia_minor
				geographical_region = custom_hungary
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arrogant
		}
	}
	
	option = { # buy the meat
		name = VIETmisc.0224.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 15
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_chamois
			years = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
	option = { # threaten the hunters to give you the meat
		name = VIETmisc.0224.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = compassionate
				has_trait = just
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					OR = {
						trait_is_sin = greedy
						trait_is_sin = callous
						trait_is_sin = sadistic
						trait_is_sin = arbitrary
					}
				}
			}
			VIET_massive_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_huge_piety_loss_effect = yes
		}
		add_dread = 10
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_eating_chamois
			years = 3
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_threatened_hunters
			years = 6
		}
		stress_impact = {
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Ok cool story bro
		name = VIETmisc.0224.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
	option = { # Share hunting tips
		name = VIETmisc.0224.d
		trigger = {
			has_trait = lifestyle_hunter
		}
		#trait = lifestyle_hunter
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			15 = { add_martial_skill = 1 }
			15 = { add_prowess_skill = 1 }
		}
		stress_impact = {
			shy = minor_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			lazy = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0224.info
		}
	}
}


# Town notable invites you to participate in caracal pigeon hunting blood sport gambling
VIETmisc.0225 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0225.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0225.desc
	theme = hunt_activity
	override_background = { event_background = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			any_county_province = {
				OR = { # Mainly seems to be a India/Central Asian phenomenon
					geographical_region = world_india
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_steppe_tarim
				}		
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = { # observe
		name = VIETmisc.0225.a
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0225.info
		}
	}
	option = { # bet on the winner
		name = VIETmisc.0225.b
		VIET_huge_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial >= decent_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial >= very_high_skill_rating
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0225.toast.good
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0225.toast.good
					random_list = {
						40 = { add_gold = 15 }
						30 = { add_gold = 25 }
						20 = { add_gold = 35 }
						10 = { add_gold = 45 }
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue <= low_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 8
					intrigue <= mediocre_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial <= low_skill_rating
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 4
					martial <= mediocre_skill_rating
				}
				desc = VIETmisc.0225.toast.bad
				send_interface_toast = {
					left_icon = ROOT
					title = VIETmisc.0225.toast.bad
					stress_impact = {
						base = minor_stress_impact_gain
						greedy = minor_stress_impact_gain
						wrathful = minor_stress_impact_gain
					}
					random_list = {
						40 = { remove_short_term_gold = 15 }
						30 = { remove_short_term_gold = 25 }
						20 = { remove_short_term_gold = 35 }
						10 = { remove_short_term_gold = 45 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0225.info
		}
	}
	option = { # have other business to take care of
		name = VIETmisc.0225.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0225.info
		}
	}
}



# Heard some yellowhammer songbird singing
VIETmisc.0226 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0226.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0226.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_tuscan_country
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = scope:courtier
		animation = happiness
	}
	right_portrait = root

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_conversion_universe_events }
		any_courtier = {
			is_available_ai_adult = yes
		}
		any_held_title = {
			tier = tier_county
			any_county_province = {
				OR = {
					geographical_region = world_europe
					geographical_region = world_asia_minor
					geographical_region = ghw_region_holy_land
					geographical_region = world_middle_east_persia
					geographical_region = world_steppe_west
					geographical_region = world_steppe_east
				}		
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_available_ai_adult = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0226.a
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0226.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0226.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_listened_to_yellowhammer
			years = 4
		}
		scope:courtier = {
			stress_impact = {
				base = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				content = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
				compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_loss
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_listened_to_yellowhammer
				years = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0226.info
		}
	}
}

			has_trait = calm
		}

			add = 0.2

		}

			add = -0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}

			add = 0.2

		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}

	}

		VIET_small_prestige_loss_effect = yes

			vengeful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0228.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0228.b
		VIET_small_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_small_piety_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = VIET_historical_context_on
			}
			custom_tooltip = VIETmisc.0228.info
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0228.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gold >= 15
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		remove_short_term_gold = 15

			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain

			NOT = { has_game_rule = VIET_normal_universe_events }
			culture_has_european_heritage_pillar_trigger = yes

		# Weed out cultures that wouldn't have these kinds of legal proceedings
		NOT = { has_government = tribal_government }
		# Wouldn't make sense for these religions

			religion = religion:judaism_religion
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
	}

	immediate = {

	}

# Butcher is giving up trade to become a wandering preacher and care for animals
VIETmisc.0230 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0230.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0230.desc
	theme = faith
	override_background = { event_background = VIET_background_small_town }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	trigger = {
		# Pick religions for which it would make sense
		OR = {
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_abrahamic }
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_eastern }
			faith = {
				OR = {
					has_doctrine = tenet_dharmic_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_reincarnation
					trait_is_sin = gluttonous
					trait_is_sin = sadistic
					trait_is_sin = callous
					trait_is_sin = wrathful
					trait_is_virtue = compassionate
					trait_is_virtue = temperate
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = gruesome_festivals_active } }
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = human_sacrifice_active } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = lazy
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0230.a
		stress_impact = {
			gregarious = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			stubborn = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0230.b
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			gluttonous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.0230.c
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			compassionate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			humble = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			temperate = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
}

# Come across a traveling cleric preaching to the animals
VIETmisc.0232 = {
	type = character_event

	override_background = { event_background = VIET_background_tuscan_country }
	
	right_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_rational
	}

	trigger = {
		# Pick religions for which it would make sense
		OR = {
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_abrahamic }
			religion = { is_in_family = rf_eastern }
			faith = {
				OR = {
					has_doctrine = tenet_dharmic_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_pacifism
					has_doctrine = tenet_mendicant_preachers
					has_doctrine = tenet_monasticism
					has_doctrine = tenet_asceticism
					has_doctrine = tenet_sanctity_of_nature
					trait_is_sin = sadistic
					trait_is_sin = callous
					trait_is_virtue = compassionate
					trait_is_virtue = generous
					trait_is_virtue = humble
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = gruesome_festivals_active } }
		NOT = { faith = { has_doctrine_parameter = human_sacrifice_active } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = calm
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = { # ok

			zealous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain

			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			sadistic = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}

		VIET_massive_prestige_loss_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_listened_to_saint_francis
			years = 10
		}
		stress_impact = {
			cynical = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			callous = medium_stress_impact_gain

			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			paranoid = minor_stress_impact_gain

# Two peasant women arguing about a patch of cabbages
VIETmisc.0234 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0234.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0234.desc
	theme = VIET_theme_small_town
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = personality_irrational
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = impatient
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = fickle
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = craven
		}
	}

	
	option = { # Tell them to shut up
		name = VIETmisc.0234.a
		VIET_medium_piety_loss_effect = yes
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			patient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			calm = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			forgiving = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}	
	option = { # Move along
		name = VIETmisc.0234.b
		stress_impact = {
			wrathful = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			impatient = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}
	}
	option = { # Help them talk it out
		name = VIETmisc.0234.c
		trigger = {
			diplomacy >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = diplomacy
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_resolved_peasant_argument
			days = 1453
		}
	}		
	option = { # Realize that animals caused it
		name = VIETmisc.0234.d
		trigger = {
			learning >= decent_skill_rating			
		}
		skill = learning
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_resolved_peasant_argument
			days = 1453
		}
	}		
}




# Notice your servant is wearing patchy clothing
VIETmisc.0235 = {
	type = character_event
	title = VIETmisc.0235.t
	desc = VIETmisc.0235.desc
	theme = unfriendly
	override_background = { event_background = corridor_day }
	
	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = disapproval
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = compassionate
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = callous
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 0.2
			has_trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -0.2
			has_trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	
	option = { # It's okay, I don't mind
		name = VIETmisc.0235.a
		VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			arrogant = minor_stress_impact_gain
			diligent = minor_stress_impact_gain
			ambitious = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}	
	
	option = { # Wear proper clothes!
		name = VIETmisc.0235.b
		VIET_medium_prestige_gain_effect = yes
		stress_impact = {
			humble = minor_stress_impact_gain
			content = minor_stress_impact_gain
			compassionate = minor_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Help her buy clothes
		name = VIETmisc.0235.c
		trigger = {
			has_trait = generous
		}
		trait = generous
		remove_short_term_gold = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				faith = {
					trait_is_virtue = generous
				}
			}
			VIET_huge_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			VIET_medium_piety_gain_effect = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = VIET_charity_to_servant
			years = 4
		}
		stress_impact = {
			callous = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
			arrogant = miniscule_stress_impact_gain
		}	
	}

}
